    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);

    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);

    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = clamp(u_xlat16_0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_10.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_10.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_10.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_10.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = clamp(u_xlat16_0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat16_0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_10.x;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat1.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = max(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = min(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_24) * u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat3.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz / u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = min(u_xlat2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat1;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

    gl_Position = u_xlat1;

    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
vec3 u_xlat11;
float u_xlat12;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_15;
mediump float u_xlat16_24;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
mediump float u_xlat16_30;
float u_xlat32;
float u_xlat33;
mediump float u_xlat16_34;
float u_xlat36;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_0.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_0.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat11.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_30);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_30) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_30 = dot((-u_xlat11.xyz), u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30 + u_xlat16_30;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_30)) + (-u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat11.xyz);
    u_xlat16_30 = abs(u_xlat16_30) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_30 = min(u_xlat16_30, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_34 = max(u_xlat16_34, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_34 = min(u_xlat16_34, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = (-u_xlat16_34) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_34 * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_4.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = exp2(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(u_xlat16_5.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_34 * u_xlat16_34;
    u_xlat11.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat16_15.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat11.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat11.x;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat11.xxx;

    u_xlat16_25 = clamp(u_xlat16_25, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-u_xlat10_1.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat10_1.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) + (-u_xlat6.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat33 = u_xlat16_0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat36 = u_xlat32 * 0.125 + u_xlat33;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat32 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat33);
    u_xlat8.y = u_xlat32 + 0.125;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat36 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat8.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * _SHColorScale.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = _SHshadow + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat32 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat32 = inversesqrt(u_xlat32);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat32) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = clamp(u_xlat2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat12 = (-u_xlat2.x) * u_xlat2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_15.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat12;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_15.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat12 = u_xlat16_34 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.z = u_xlat16_34 + 1.0;
    u_xlat2.xz = u_xlat2.xz * u_xlat2.xz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat12;
    u_xlat2.x = min(u_xlat2.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xxx * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = clamp(u_xlat33, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyw * vec3(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = u_xlat2.xyw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = min(u_xlat16_7.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat2.xyw * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xxx + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_15.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = clamp(u_xlat16_15.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyw * u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = max(u_xlat16_15.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = min(u_xlat16_15.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat16_4.xyw + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.z * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_15.x = (-u_xlat2.z) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_15.x + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat16_30 = u_xlat16_30 / u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_15.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.x = dot(u_xlat16_15.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_0.x = clamp(u_xlat16_0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_30 * u_xlat16_0.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_10.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_10.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_10.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_10.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = clamp(u_xlat16_0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_10.x = u_xlat16_0.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x;
    u_xlat16_0.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_10.x;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * u_xlat16_0.xxx;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = max(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = min(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_24) * u_xlat10_1.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_1.w;
    return;
}

in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;

vec4 u_xlat0;

float u_xlat14;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat2;

    u_xlat13 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

    return;

        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati25).z + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati25).w;
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat37 = u_xlat37 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_26) * _AdditionalLightsColorDynamicIndex(u_xlati25).xyz;
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat37) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
        u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    }
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz / u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat2.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat2.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat14 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat14 = max(u_xlat14, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat14 = inversesqrt(u_xlat14);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat14) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.w = u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat13 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat13 = max(u_xlat13, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat13 = inversesqrt(u_xlat13);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat13) * u_xlat3.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
uint u_xlatu1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
vec2 u_xlat9;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_9;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
vec3 u_xlat13;
uint u_xlatu13;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
float u_xlat17;
vec3 u_xlat20;
float u_xlat25;
int u_xlati25;
bool u_xlatb25;
mediump float u_xlat16_26;
float u_xlat32;
float u_xlat37;
bool u_xlatb37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
float u_xlat41;
mediump float u_xlat16_42;
float u_xlat43;
mediump float u_xlat16_46;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_14) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14 = min(max(u_xlat16_14, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_14 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14 = min(max(u_xlat16_14, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat8.xyz, u_xlat8.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat13.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = abs(u_xlat16_4.x) + 0.00400000019;

        u_xlat24 = float(u_xlati_loop_1);
        u_xlatb1 = u_xlat24<2.0;

        u_xlat24 = (u_xlatb1) ? u_xlat24 : u_xlat13.x;

        u_xlati24 = int(u_xlat16_26);
        u_xlat1.xyz = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz) + _AdditionalLightsPositionDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).xyz;

        u_xlat37 = max(u_xlat37, 6.10351563e-05);
        u_xlat5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat37);
        u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * u_xlat5.xxx;
        u_xlat5.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat37;
        u_xlat37 = u_xlat37 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).x + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).y;
        u_xlat37 = clamp(u_xlat37, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat37 = u_xlat37 * u_xlat5.x;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(_AdditionalLightsSpotDirDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).z + _AdditionalLightsAttenuationDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).w;
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat37 = u_xlat37 * u_xlat16_26;
        u_xlat16_26 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
        u_xlat16_26 = clamp(u_xlat16_26, 0.0, 1.0);
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_26) * _AdditionalLightsColorDynamicIndex(u_xlati24).xyz;
        u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat37) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
        u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    }
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w;
    return;
}

mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;

int u_xlati24;
bool u_xlatb24;

mediump float u_xlat16_26;

mediump float u_xlat16_39;

mediump float u_xlat16_42;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(abs(u_xlat16_1.z));
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_1.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_1.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_2.z = max(u_xlat16_26, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_2.xz = min(u_xlat16_2.xz, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_1.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_3.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_4.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_4.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat13.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_14) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_39 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14 = min(max(u_xlat16_14, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-u_xlat16_0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_14) + u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_14 = (-u_xlat16_2.z) + u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_14 = u_xlat16_14 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_14 = min(max(u_xlat16_14, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_14 = clamp(u_xlat16_14, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_2.z * u_xlat16_2.z;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;

in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
bool u_xlatb10;
float u_xlat11;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_12;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_22;
mediump float u_xlat16_25;
float u_xlat31;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
float u_xlat34;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
float u_xlat37;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat1.xy,u_xlat1.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_12.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb10 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb10 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb10 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_2.x + _SHshadow;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_12.x = min(max(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_12.x = clamp(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_22.xy = u_xlat16_3.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_22.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat16_22.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyw;
    u_xlat16_22.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_22.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22.x = dot((-u_xlat10.xyz), u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = u_xlat16_22.x + u_xlat16_22.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * (-u_xlat16_22.xxx) + (-u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = abs(u_xlat16_22.x) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_0.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_22.y = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_22.xy = min(u_xlat16_22.xy, vec2(1.0, 1.0));
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_22.y) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_22.y * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_4 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_4.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_33 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = max(u_xlat16_33, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = log2(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_33 = exp2(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = log2(abs(u_xlat16_0.z));
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * _AOScale;
    u_xlat16_33 = exp2(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = min(u_xlat16_33, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_33) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_22.y * u_xlat16_22.y;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat10.x = (-u_xlat16_22.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_22.x = (-u_xlat16_22.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat10.x * u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_0.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_0.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_15) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_15;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_6.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6.x = (-u_xlat16_22.y) + u_xlat16_6.x;
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_6.x + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_15) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_15) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xxx + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * u_xlat8.xyz + u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat16_3.y * u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat34 = u_xlat16_3.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat37 = u_xlat31 * 0.125 + u_xlat34;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat34);
    u_xlat8.y = u_xlat31 + 0.125;
    u_xlat8.x = u_xlat37 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_5.xy = max(u_xlat8.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_5.xy = u_xlat16_5.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * _SHColorScale.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_33) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat31 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat31);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat31) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat1.x = min(max(u_xlat1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat11 = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_35 / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_22.y * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.z = u_xlat16_22.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xz = u_xlat1.xz * u_xlat1.xz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat34 = min(max(u_xlat34, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat34 = clamp(u_xlat34, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw * vec3(u_xlat34);
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = vec3(u_xlat34) * u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);

    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_33) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat31 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat31);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat31) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = clamp(u_xlat1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat11 = (-u_xlat1.x) * u_xlat1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat11;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_35 / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat11 = u_xlat16_22.y * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat1.z = u_xlat16_22.y + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.xz = u_xlat1.xz * u_xlat1.xz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat11;
    u_xlat1.x = min(u_xlat1.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat34 = clamp(u_xlat34, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw * vec3(u_xlat34);
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = vec3(u_xlat34) * u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat1.xyw * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = u_xlat16_5.xyw * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xxx + u_xlat16_5.xyw;
    u_xlat16_12.x = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_12.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_12.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_12.x = clamp(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xxx * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyw * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = max(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = min(u_xlat16_6.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = u_xlat16_5.xyw + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.z * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_12.x = (-u_xlat1.z) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_22.x * u_xlat16_12.x + u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_22.x / u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_22.x = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22.x);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_22.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22.x = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22.x = clamp(u_xlat16_22.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_22.x = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_22.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_22.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_22.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_22.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_22.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_22.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = clamp(u_xlat16_12.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_22.x = u_xlat16_12.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_12.x = u_xlat16_12.x * u_xlat16_22.x;
    u_xlat16_22.x = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_22.x + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_12.x;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat10_0.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_12.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_12.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_12.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = min(u_xlat16_2.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyw;
    SV_Target0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat10_0.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat10_0.w;
    return;
}

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy * vec2(vec2(_FurTilling, _FurTilling));
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

        u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);

    u_xlat0.xyz = min(u_xlat1.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));

    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-_OutlineColor.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat3.xyz + _OutlineColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = textureLod(_OutlineMap, in_TEXCOORD0.xy, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD1.w = u_xlat1.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_NORMAL0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_NORMAL0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_NORMAL0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xz = u_xlat0.yy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].xy * u_xlat0.xx + u_xlat3.xz;
    u_xlat0.xy = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].xy * u_xlat0.zz + u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat6) * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy / _ScreenParams.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * _ScreenResolution.yy;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat1.y * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1].w;
    u_xlat6 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0].w * u_xlat1.x + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat6 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2].w * u_xlat1.z + u_xlat6;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3].w;
    u_xlat0.xy = vec2(u_xlat6) * u_xlat0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(0.00462962966, 0.00462962966);
    u_xlat2.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat2.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].y;
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy / u_xlat2.xy;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat1.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].xyz * u_xlat1.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].xyz * u_xlat1.zzz + u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xy = u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat1.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat0.xy);
    u_xlat0.x = sqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat3.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat3.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat3.x);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xxx * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz / abs(u_xlat3.zzz);
    u_xlat10 = abs(_Offset) * 0.150000006;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 100.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].z;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].z;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].z;
    u_xlat1.w = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].z;
    u_xlat0.w = 1.0;
    gl_Position.z = dot(u_xlat1, u_xlat0);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[0].x;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].x;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].x;
    gl_Position.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[1].y;
    u_xlat1.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].y;
    u_xlat1.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].y;
    gl_Position.y = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.yzw);
    u_xlat0.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[2].w;
    u_xlat0.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4glstate_matrix_projection[3].w;
    gl_Position.w = dot(u_xlat0.xy, u_xlat0.zw);
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
void main()
{
    SV_Target0.xyz = max(vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    SV_Target0.w = vs_TEXCOORD1.w;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
